{"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_01DW9GebPXGnJfgpeS5gFuCn","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_019BuES7aLGDnep6w7ZjyczN","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/torch/optim/gradient_noise.py","content":"# mypy: allow-untyped-defs\nr\"\"\"Implementation for Gradient Noise Injection optimizer wrapper.\"\"\"\n\nfrom typing import Optional, Union\n\nimport torch\nfrom torch import Tensor\n\nfrom .optimizer import Optimizer\n\n\n__all__ = [\"GradientNoiseInjector\"]\n\n\nclass GradientNoiseInjector:\n    r\"\"\"Wraps an optimizer to inject calibrated Gaussian noise into gradients.\n\n    Implements the \"Adding Gradient Noise Improves Learning for Very Deep Networks\"\n    technique. Noise is injected into each gradient before the optimizer step,\n    with variance following a decreasing schedule.\n\n    Args:\n        optimizer (Optimizer): the optimizer to wrap\n        eta (float, optional): noise schedule scaling parameter (default: 0.01)\n        gamma (float, optional): noise schedule decay exponent (default: 0.55)\n\n    Example:\n        >>> base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        >>> optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n        >>> for epoch in range(num_epochs):\n        >>>     for batch in dataloader:\n        >>>         optimizer.zero_grad()\n        >>>         loss = model(batch)\n        >>>         loss.backward()\n        >>>         optimizer.step()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        optimizer: Optimizer,\n        eta: float = 0.01,\n        gamma: float = 0.55,\n    ) -> None:\n        if not isinstance(optimizer, Optimizer):\n            raise TypeError(f\"{type(optimizer).__name__} is not an Optimizer\")\n        if eta < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid eta value: {eta}\")\n        if gamma < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid gamma value: {gamma}\")\n\n        self.optimizer = optimizer\n        self.eta = eta\n        self.gamma = gamma\n        self.step_count = 0\n\n    def __getattr__(self, name: str):\n        \"\"\"Delegate attribute access to the wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        return getattr(self.optimizer, name)\n\n    def __setattr__(self, name: str, value) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Delegate attribute setting to wrapped optimizer for most attributes.\"\"\"\n        if name in [\"optimizer\", \"eta\", \"gamma\", \"step_count\"]:\n            # These are attributes of the wrapper itself\n            super().__setattr__(name, value)\n        else:\n            # Delegate to wrapped optimizer\n            setattr(self.optimizer, name, value)\n\n    def step(self, closure: Optional[callable] = None) -> Optional[Tensor]:\n        r\"\"\"Performs a single optimization step with gradient noise injection.\n\n        Args:\n            closure (Callable, optional): A closure that reevaluates the model\n                and returns the loss.\n\n        Returns:\n            The loss value if closure is not None, otherwise None.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Inject Gaussian noise into gradients\n        self._inject_noise()\n\n        # Call the base optimizer's step\n        loss = self.optimizer.step(closure)\n\n        # Increment step counter\n        self.step_count += 1\n\n        return loss\n\n    def _inject_noise(self) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Inject calibrated Gaussian noise into model gradients.\n\n        Noise variance follows the schedule: sigma^2 = eta / (1 + t)^gamma\n        where t is the step count.\n        \"\"\"\n        # Calculate noise variance for this step\n        sigma_squared = self.eta / ((1.0 + self.step_count) ** self.gamma)\n        sigma = sigma_squared ** 0.5\n\n        # Inject noise into each parameter group\n        for group in self.optimizer.param_groups:\n            for param in group[\"params\"]:\n                if param.grad is not None:\n                    # Add Gaussian noise to gradient\n                    noise = torch.randn_like(param.grad) * sigma\n                    param.grad.add_(noise)\n\n    def zero_grad(self, set_to_none: bool = False) -> None:\n        r\"\"\"Clear the gradients of all optimized parameters.\n\n        Args:\n            set_to_none (bool, optional): instead of setting to zero, set the\n                grads to None. Noise is injected into each gradient before the optimizer step,\n    with variance following a decreasing schedule.\n\n    Args:\n        optimizer (Optimizer): the optimizer to wrap\n        eta (float, optional): noise schedule scaling parameter (default: 0.01)\n        gamma (float, optional): noise schedule decay exponent (default: 0.55)\n\n    Example:\n        >>> base_optimizer = SGD(model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        >>> optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n        >>> for epoch in range(num_epochs):\n        >>>     for batch in dataloader:\n        >>>         optimizer.zero_grad()\n        >>>         loss = model(batch)\n        >>>         loss.backward()\n        >>>         optimizer.step()\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def __init__(\n        self,\n        optimizer: Optimizer,\n        eta: float = 0.01,\n        gamma: float = 0.55,\n    ) -> None:\n        if not isinstance(optimizer, Optimizer):\n            raise TypeError(f\"{type(optimizer).__name__} is not an Optimizer\")\n        if eta < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid eta value: {eta}\")\n        if gamma < 0.0:\n            raise ValueError(f\"Invalid gamma value: {gamma}\")\n\n        self.optimizer = optimizer\n        self.eta = eta\n        self.gamma = gamma\n        self.step_count = 0\n\n    def __getattr__(self, name: str):\n        \"\"\"Delegate attribute access to the wrapped optimizer.\"\"\"\n        return getattr(self.optimizer, name)\n\n    def __setattr__(self, name: str, value) -> None:\n        \"\"\"Delegate attribute setting to wrapped optimizer for most attributes.\"\"\"\n        if name in [\"optimizer\", \"eta\", \"gamma\", \"step_count\"]:\n            # Forward, backward, and step\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            loss = self.criterion(self.model(x), y)\n            loss.backward()\n            optimizer.step()\n\n        # Check that step_count incremented properly\n        self.assertEqual(optimizer.step_count, 5)\n\n    def test_step_counter_increments(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that step counter increments correctly.\"\"\"\n        base_optimizer = SGD(self.model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        y = torch.randn(5, 1)\n\n        self.assertEqual(optimizer.step_count, 0)\n\n        for expected_step in range(1, 6):\n            optimizer.zero_grad()\n            loss = self.criterion(self.model(x), y)\n            loss.backward()\n            optimizer.step()\n            self.assertEqual(optimizer.step_count, expected_step)\n\n    def test_zero_grad_delegation(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that zero_grad properly delegates to base optimizer.\"\"\"\n        base_optimizer = SGD(self.model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        y = torch.randn(5, 1)\n\n        # Create gradients\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\n        loss = self.criterion(self.model(x), y)\n        loss.backward()\n\n        # Verify gradients exist\n        for p in self.model.parameters():\n            if p.grad is not None:\n                self.assertFalse(torch.all(p.grad == 0))\n\n        # Zero gradients\n        optimizer.zero_grad()\n\n        # Verify gradients are zeroed\n        for p in self.model.parameters():\n            if p.grad is not None:\n                self.assertTrue(torch.all(p.grad == 0))\n\n    def test_state_dict_save_load(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that state can be saved and loaded.\"\"\"\n        base_optimizer = SGD(self.model.parameters(), lr=0.1)\n        optimizer = GradientNoiseInjector(base_optimizer, eta=0.01, gamma=0.55)\n\n        x = torch.randn(5, 10)\n        y = torch.randn(5, 1)\n\n        # Use larger eta to make noise effect obvious\n            gamma=0.55,\n        )\n        opt_noise.zero_grad()\n        loss1 = self.criterion(model_with_noise(x), y)\n        loss1.backward()\n        opt_noise.step()\n\n        #
